Fire in Jia Le Road; Four Deaths Burned to Death; Shi Wenbao and Two Sons Died While Visiting Relatives; Corpses with Broken Limbs and Legs, Gruesome to Look At 153

The report that the house at No. 198, Lane 2, Yongxing Alley, Jia Le Road, French Concession, was rented to a second landlord as a workshop for manufacturing imitation jade and rosin combs, and a fire broke out the night before due to worker negligence, causing the owner and workers to escape on the spot and burning people to death, was briefly recorded in yesterday's newspaper. It is now known that the second landlord of the house is Shi Zengqing from Jiaxing, 44 years old this year, who has been a waiter at the Huizhong Hotel for many years. In addition to living on the floor above, he recently rented the common room downstairs to an unknown jade rosin craft workshop. Recently, Shi Wenbao (32 years old from Jiaxing, wife of Shi Shaoshan, Shi's uncle), who had been inquired from his hometown, came to Shanghai three or four days ago with his eldest son Shi Qiaoguan, 9 years old, and his youngest son Hui Bao, 3 years old, to visit Shi Zengqing and his wife, temporarily residing in the back loft of the common room. When the fire broke out the night before, Shi and his wife were already asleep upstairs. Shi Wenfei, his two sons, and Zengqing's cousin Shi Qingbao, a total of four people, were also asleep. When the fire broke out, the owner and workers of the workshop who caused the fire all fled to avoid punishment. Shi Qingzeng and his wife jumped out of the upstairs window. Shi Qingbao and Shi Wenbao woke up from their dreams. Wenbao immediately took his two sons downstairs to avoid the fire and entered the kitchen shed. Because the house had no back door, and the fire blocked the door and burned, Shi Qingbao, Shi Wenbao, Shi Qiaoguan, and Shi Huibao, a total of four people, could not escape and died together in the fire. Afterwards, the Fire Brigade pulled out the corpses of Shi Qingbao, Shi Wenbao, and Shi Huibao. They had broken limbs and legs, ruptured abdomens and flowing intestines, and looked like charred wood, which was gruesome to look at. The police sent detectives to carry the corpses to the Tongren Fuyuan Sub-hall autopsy station, and brought the second landlord Shi Qingzeng to the case for questioning. Yesterday, the Criminal Court's Procuratorate was requested to dispatch ten prosecutors, including forensic doctor Wei and clerk Peng, to the station for inspection. The family member Shi Shaoshan arrived at the scene to identify the corpses. After the autopsy, he sat on the public case. According to the investigation report of detective Zhang Chunsheng, the officials interrogated Shi Qingzeng and Shi Shaoshan. They then ordered that the corpses of Shi Qingbin, Shi Wenbin, and Shi Huibao were indeed burned to death during their lifetimes, and the corpses were handed over to Shi Qingzeng and others to collect the corpses separately. The arsonist or arsonists will be arrested by the police department for investigation and interrogation. As for Shi Qingzeng's wife, who was slightly injured when she jumped down, she went to the hospital for treatment. The police are now sending detectives to investigate the fire starter and bring them to justice for interrogation. The corpse of Shi Qiaoguan was pulled out by the Fire Brigade at 2:00 PM yesterday afternoon and taken to the autopsy station, waiting for today's autopsy report.

After Xu Yabo's Death, Concubine Sues for Property Division; First Wife's Side Claims Ignorance; Plaintiff Presents Identity Proof 154

Xu Yabo, from Hubei, was the former district chief of the First Jiangsu Water Police District stationed in Minhang. After his resignation, he lived in Shanghai as a retired official. Several years ago, he was implicated in the robbery case of the notorious bandit Tai Bao Ashu, who had already been captured. After repeated appeals, he was finally declared innocent and returned to Shanghai to reside at No. 254 Juji Da Road in the French Concession. Due to his inner turmoil, he fell ill and passed away in April of this year despite medical treatment. Recently, Xu Lu Qiuyun, Xu Yabo's concubine residing at No. 497 Xin Dagu Road, along with her three sons, jointly filed a lawsuit in the Civil Court through a lawyer against Xu Wangshi, Xu's legal wife, seeking a division of property. The lawsuit stated that the legal representative, Xu Lu Qiuyun, at the age of fifteen, was seduced and defiled by Xu Yabo, who then took her as his concubine and housed her separately. The plaintiffs in this case, Xu Boli, Xu BoWei, and Xu Bosheng, were born from this union. All their living expenses were borne by Xu Yabo. Unfortunately, Xu Yabo passed away in April of this year. The defendant, Xu Wangshi, as Xu Yabo's legal wife, has completely seized all the inheritance, causing the plaintiff and her sons to live in great hardship. As co-heirs of Xu Yabo, they are suffering from unequal distribution of wealth. It is discovered that Xu Yabo owned properties during his lifetime, such as the "Ya Residence" in Minhang, land and houses in Zhuji, and cash, totaling 70,000 yuan. Xu Yabo's first wife had a daughter, and the defendant also had two sons. Together with the plaintiff's brothers and sister, there are seven heirs in total. The inheritance should be divided into seven shares, each share being 10,000 yuan. The plaintiff should receive 30,000 yuan. They request the court to order the surrender and distribution of the inheritance, etc. The court approved the case. Yesterday morning at 10:30, Judge Ma Yishu summoned both the plaintiff and the defendant in Civil Court No. 7. Both parties were represented by lawyers. First, the plaintiff's lawyer presented the case and stated a request to change the object of the lawsuit, dividing the 70,000 yuan inheritance into eight shares, including the defendant Xu Wangshi as one share. The three plaintiffs should jointly receive more than 16,000 yuan of the inheritance, etc. The defendant's lawyer, Xu Yannian, responded that the defendant was completely unaware that Xu Yabo had another concubine and children during his lifetime. Even if it were true, Xu Yabo's financial situation was dire after his discharge, burdened with debts. He was falsely accused of conspiring in a robbery case during his lifetime. When he was acquitted and released from prison, he borrowed money and rice from others, and there are letters that can prove this. As for the Ya Residence, it is only worth three or four thousand yuan, but it has already been mortgaged to the wife of Shen Baoyi. There is no other inheritance. He requested that the plaintiff's lawsuit be dismissed, etc. At this point, the plaintiff's lawyer presented photos of Xu Yabo with the plaintiff and school certificates, with Xu Yabo listed as the parent, which can prove the identity of the plaintiffs. The court verified the evidence and instructed both lawyers to debate the case before announcing the conclusion and scheduling the verdict for the afternoon of the 20th.

A Thousand Days of Thieving, There Will Surely Be a Day of Exposure: Li Zhangyu Specializes in Stealing Car Parts for Retail; Sentenced to Two Years and Six Months After the Case Was Cracked 155

Li Zhangyu, a local, used to be a chauffeur. Since losing his job, he specialized in stealing car parts. His methods were clever and always successful. He made a living this way in both the British and French Concessions, with more than eleven households being victims of his thefts. The stolen car parts included car bells, horns, air pumps, angle irons, and other items. As the saying goes, "A thousand days of thieving, there will surely be a day of exposure." On the 12th of this month, he was caught near the intersection of Avenue Joffre and Route Dufour by Chinese Detective Shen Dehui of the Municipal Police and sent to the First Special District Court for investigation. During the investigation, it was discovered that between October 3rd of last year and June 11th of this year, he had stolen parts from cars belonging to: (1) a Westerner at No. 987 Tibet Road; (2) a Westerner at No. 1677 Avenue Haig; (3) a Westerner at the western end of Xin Zha Road near Hardoon Road; (4) a Westerner near the intersection of Avenue Joffre and Route Dufour; (5) a Westerner at No. 1187 Connaught Road; (6) Tang Shixuan, a Chinese resident of the French Concession outside Xiaoshadu Road No. 336; (7) Shi Yucun, a Chinese resident of No. 1087 Dagu Road; (8) Yao Jiakun, a Chinese resident of No. 1564 Xin Zha Road; (9) Xin Yaoyang, a Chinese resident of No. 3 Route Dufour; (10) a Westerner near the small vegetable market on Boone Road; (11) a Westerner near the Racecourse on Route Say Zo. The stolen parts were worth more than 400 yuan, which he spent. Yesterday, Judge Liu Yugui presided over the Eighth Criminal Court and clearly questioned him. Li Zhangyu was sentenced to two years and six months of imprisonment. The number of days of detention before the judgment was finalized will be deducted from the prison term at a rate of one day for one day. He was also allowed to be taken by the Special Second District Court police. After the interrogation, he was sent back to serve his sentence.

The Chinese Association for the Protection of Children Sends Out Proposals for the International Federation for Home Education; Five Proposals Have Been Sent to Representative Ding in Geneva 156

From July 31st to August 4th of this year, the Fifth International Home Education Conference of the International Federation for Home Education will be held in Brussels, the capital of Belgium, to discuss and promote international home education matters. The Chinese Association for the Protection of Children has selected Ding Shujing as its representative to attend the conference. She departed for Europe on the 15th to first represent the Chinese Young Women's Christian Association (YWCA) at the executive committee meeting of the World YWCA in Geneva. After the meeting, she will go directly to Brussels to represent the Chinese Association for the Protection of Children at the Fifth International Home Education Conference. According to a reporter's inquiry yesterday, the Chinese Association for the Protection of Children has printed a beautifully illustrated pamphlet describing the association's work, for reference by relevant parties. They have also written a paper titled "Home Education in China" in English, describing China as a country that values family education, with countless virtuous mothers and righteous women throughout history, as well as the progress of new China in the field of home education, so that Representative Ding can read it at the conference and have it published in newspapers in various countries, so that people from various countries can understand the state of home education in China. In addition to the above English publicity brochure and English paper, the Chinese Association for the Protection of Children has also drafted the following five proposals for the conference: (1) In the future, the highest goal of home education in all countries of the world should be to "train children to be world citizens" (including understanding and respect for other races and other countries, as well as the virtues of striving for lofty ideals for mankind), in order to sweep away the darkness of the past world and establish the light of the original world. (2) The International Federation for Home Education should publish a periodical to promote home education in all countries of the world, and to enable parents in various countries to recognize each other, exchange opinions, understand each other's special problems, and the special methods to deal with these special problems. (3) The International Federation for Home Education should establish branches in various countries of the world to assist the General Assembly in completing its great achievements. (4) In the history of various countries in the world, we often find the handsome and wise faces of great parents. For example, in the history of the Hebrew nation, there are the mothers of Moses, Samuel, and Jesus. In the history of the Chinese nation, there are the mothers of Ji Chang (King Wen of Zhou), Mencius, and Yue Fei. All these people were able to cultivate virtuous children with their painstaking efforts and make significant contributions to mankind. The International Federation for Home Education should appoint a number of committees to collect the stories of great parents of this kind from various countries and compile them into "Biographies of Great Parents of the World" to distribute to various countries for parents to admire and emulate. (5) The International Federation for Home Education should at any time praise the achievements and express gratitude for the efforts of great fathers (who can train their children to become world citizens with painstaking efforts and make significant and special contributions to the world and mankind) in the modern world. All the above items have been compiled by Xu Jianping, the general secretary of the association, and sent to Geneva, Switzerland, yesterday, and handed over to Representative Ding Shujing for use at the meeting on July 31st.

Jianghai Customs Proclamation: Banning the Private Purchase of Banknote Paper; All Purchases Will Be Detained and Submitted to the Ministry for Review 160

It must not be released privately. You must comply accordingly," etc. Having received this, we must comply. All merchants are hereby notified. This proclamation is hereby issued.

Samsung Rickshaw Company Trials Passenger Pick-Up and Drop-Off at the North Station; Formal Contract Has Been Signed by Both Parties; to be Implemented from July 1st for a One-Year Term 163

Xin Xin News reports that the Shanghai North Station pick-up and drop-off service for passengers has already been contracted to Xiang Sheng Motors. However, rickshaw pullers also hoped to contract for the service. After the Transportation Department studied the matter for a long time, it was approved by the Railway Bureau to be tentatively contracted to the Shanghai Samsung Rickshaw Company. A contract was signed, and it will be implemented starting July 1st of this year for a one-year term. The contract is excerpted as follows:

The Railway Bureau Approves the Contract

(1) The Railway Bureau allows the contractor to use rickshaws to conduct passenger pick-up and drop-off at the Shanghai North Station on a trial basis. This contractual right may not be transferred. If there is a transfer, the contractual right will be revoked. (2) The rickshaw fare will be based on the zoning of the Shanghai map and will be agreed upon and announced by both parties. After it is set, any changes must be approved by the Railway Bureau. The contractor may not unilaterally decide to implement them. (3) The fare in the rickshaw fare table includes the rickshaw puller's work of picking up and dropping off passengers' luggage and accompanying them onto and off the rickshaw, and must send them to the entrance of the lane where the passenger wants to go. (4) The "silver dime" mentioned in the rickshaw fare table is generally taken to mean the big

Page 12

dollar. The "points" mentioned will be converted according to the market price, and the price may not be raised. (5) If the rickshaw fare needs to be revised, the original fare will still apply before the new fare is announced. (6) Regardless of day or night, sunshine or rain, cold or warm, and the amount of luggage, the fare will be calculated according to the regulations. Rickshaw pullers are not allowed to make any demands. (7) Passengers hire rickshaws and purchase rickshaw tickets at the ticket sales point designated by the Railway Bureau. The "destination," "fare," "date," etc. will be filled in by the staff hired by the contractor, and the contractor will pay for the ticket printing. The first and second copies should be given to the passenger, and the third copy will be kept as a receipt for the Railway Bureau to check at any time. When the passenger arrives at the destination, the first copy will be given to the rickshaw puller as the fare, and the rickshaw puller will return it to the contractor. The passenger will keep the second copy in case they forget something on the rickshaw or the rickshaw puller makes extortionate demands, so that they can be investigated. (8) Rickshaws entering the station will be issued a free license by the Railway Bureau as proof. The number of rickshaws will be determined according to needs. (9) If there are not enough rickshaws, the contractor must hire rickshaws from other companies. They may not refuse passengers due to lack of rickshaws. Rickshaws hired from other companies will still be charged according to the prescribed fare and payment method.

Guaranteed Responsibilities

(10) The contractor's responsibilities and guarantees are as follows: (A) If the rickshaw puller makes extortionate demands from passengers or engages in other illegal acts, the rickshaw puller will be ordered to return the amount demanded or hand over the rickshaw puller for legal action. (B) If passengers forget something on the rickshaw, the rickshaw puller will be ordered to send it to the Railway Bureau for lost and found or hand over the rickshaw puller for legal action. (C) All staff, foremen, and rickshaw pullers dispatched will not engage in improper behavior and will be subject to the direction of Railway Bureau personnel. (D) Rickshaws will be assigned to hire passengers in order and may not scramble for customers or disrupt order. (E) When trains arrive, foremen must be on duty at the station day and night in shifts. (F) Vehicles must be clean. (G) The foremen on duty at the station and the rickshaw pullers hired should wear uniforms of the style prescribed by the Railway Bureau, and the contractor will pay for the uniforms. (H) No money may be given to any Railway Bureau employee or railway police officer. (I) All Railway Bureau regulations must be observed. (11) The Railway Bureau will issue rickshaw licenses free of charge and provide a location for issuing rickshaw tickets. This location should be designated by the Railway Bureau. If any equipment needs to be installed, the contractor will draw up a plan and submit it to the Railway Bureau for approval. The contractor will be responsible for the installation costs. If the Railway Bureau needs to use the designated location, the contractor must move it immediately and may not object. (12) The contractor shall pay a deposit of 300 yuan to the Railway Bureau and provide a guarantee to ensure that the contractor fulfills the terms of the contract. If there is a violation of the terms, the Railway Bureau may dispose of the deposit according to the severity of the violation. If the contract expires and the contractor has no obligations to fulfill under the contract, they may recover the deposit from the Railway Bureau with a receipt. The interest on the deposit will be determined by the chief accountant of the Railway Bureau. If the guarantor of the guarantee relocates or goes out of business, the contractor must notify the Railway Bureau and change the guarantor. Failure to report will be considered a violation of the contract. (13) If the contractor does not manage the business well, and the Railway Bureau believes that it is necessary to terminate the contract, the contract will be invalid upon notification. (14) This trial contract will be valid from July 1, 1935 to June 30, 1936. If both parties agree at the end of the trial period, the contractor will have priority in signing a formal contract.

He is kind and amiable to passengers, and his colleagues get along well with him. Therefore, he is highly valued by the Westerners in the company, and his colleagues have always praised him. He recently submitted his resignation, and the company initially tried to retain him, but because of his firm intention to resign, they had to approve it and specially inscribed the words "Success and Fame" to commemorate him. When his colleagues heard the news, they felt a sense of loss. Therefore, Yang Meinan, the Chinese director, Yang Shaonan, the manager, and colleagues Chen Jiechu and Zhang Zhipan, as well as the Customs Brokers Association, initiated a public banquet for Mr. Yang last night (the 20th) at the Atlantic Restaurant on 4th Avenue. More than 100 colleagues from the company and representatives of various passengers attended, and the atmosphere was lively and bustling. During the banquet, Mr. Chen Jiechu first reported the purpose of the meeting, and then Yang Meinan gave a speech, describing Mr. Yang Dongming's history of service at Taikoo. Golden City Photo Studio also took photos to commemorate the occasion. Everyone enjoyed themselves and dispersed.

A Record of the Trial of the Rent Reduction Case in Baoyu Lane 166

Baoxing Lane in Zhabei's Baoxing Road is surrounded by desolation, and the rent is expensive. The full details of the tenants' requests for rent reduction have been recorded in this newspaper. At 1:30 PM yesterday, another hearing was held. Forty-five tenants attended, represented by lawyers Yu Hualong and Chen Yi and agents Hu Yukang and Sheng Ruji. They immediately stated that the rents in the vicinity are lower. The cost and land price of Baoxing Lane are calculated to have a strong interest rate of 1.8%, which is difficult to bear due to such heavy exploitation. The market is declining and people's livelihoods are declining. They requested that the court order a 30% rent reduction. The judge asked the representative of the defendant, the Tongfu Company, lawyer Huang, how much the land price was and how many rooms could be built per mu. Huang replied that the Zhabei market is becoming more prosperous every day. As soon as a room is built, it will immediately open for business. The land price of Baoxing Lane is 30,000 yuan per mu, and 11 shikumen rooms can be built per mu. However, the tenants were enraged when they heard Huang's exaggerated words. Because they had to maintain order in court, they could not question him. After the court adjourned and went to the lawyers' lounge, the tenants asked lawyer Huang why he had exaggerated the Zhabei market to such an extent. The judge also asked because the defendant's lawyer Huang's answers were excessive. A reinvestigation will be carried out after a personal investigation.

West Shanghai Hongqiao Road Robbery 169

Last night around 11 PM, at the home of Huang Xitang, a Pudong native, residing at No. 13 Xujiazhai, north of Yanjiabridge, east of the Hongqiao Airport in West Shanghai, eight robbers speaking a dialect, wearing blue cloth short shirts and trousers, suddenly broke through the door. Four of the robbers each held a pistol. Huang's entire family was startled awake from their dreams, and their hands were tied behind their backs with ropes by the robbers, forbidding them to make a sound. The robbers overturned chests and cabinets, searching at will, and made off with approximately twenty-one silver dollars, one gold ring, one gold watch, and clothing worth over two hundred dollars. After about twenty minutes, they howled and departed westward. The victim reported the incident to Officer Wang Zhizhang, Police Chief Zhao Yuren of the Chengjiaqiao police station in charge. Upon receiving the report, they personally led all the police officers and joined the Pu-Song District Security Corps to search in different directions. At that time, it was pouring rain, and the roads were muddy and slippery. Moreover, the distance was four or five *li*. By the time the corps and police arrived, the robbers had long vanished without a trace.

Fire on Fangbin Road Yesterday, Destroyed Three Floors, Fire Starter Taken for Questioning 170

Zhang Asong, a 46-year-old Suzhou native, has been running Zhang Ji Board/Brush Wholesale Shop at No. 372 Fangbin Road in the city for over ten years. Zhang's wife, Ms. Yu, and their children live upstairs, while fourteen employees and apprentices live downstairs. Unexpectedly, at 2:10 AM yesterday morning, Zhang's wife, Ms. Yu, got up for something and was about to turn on the light switch on the bed when the light suddenly short-circuited and caught fire. Instantly, thick smoke filled the air, and the flames blazed fiercely, piercing through the roof. Nearby patrol officers, upon learning of the fire, immediately notified the fire brigades of each district by telephone. Quickly, pump and hose trucks rushed to the scene. The firefighters worked hard to extinguish the fire, and it was finally extinguished in about an hour. The fire destroyed two floors of the shop at No. 372 and spread to one floor of the neighboring Ye Shengxing Rattan Shop at No. 374, causing significant losses. At the time, neighbors nearby were moving and grabbing boxes of items, helping the old and carrying the young, fleeing in a great panic. The situation was extremely chaotic. Director Shen Zhenhua led the police to maintain order and investigate the cause of the fire, taking the fire starter, Zhang A'gen, to the station for questioning. It is said that Zhang Ji Board/Brush Shop had taken out fire insurance with a certain insurance company for two thousand dollars.

Yesterday afternoon, Judge He Jingxian summoned all the creditors, totaling 124, all of whom brought account books to court to verify the amount of money owed. Spring and Autumn

Tidbits 184

— (Wu Jiren)

A small boat heavily loaded will eventually be unable to withstand the strong winds and waves. A sudden gust of wind will cause the boat to sway and capsize. It all depends on the helmsman's care; otherwise, capsizing will follow.

A scholar dies for one who understands him. The ancients said that one should not regret dying if one has a true friend. In the vast sea of dust, who can truly be called a true friend? Daily, I am with my shadow, and my shadow is with me.

"Once power is in hand, one should issue orders." Life is like morning dew. Do not miss the good opportunity in this one morning, this one moment when you are in command. It will be too late to regret it after death. Therefore, life is about "doing what is timely." (Fictitious Chen quote.)

Playing mahjong, "Pure One Suit" can be counted as three points. However, to get a "Pure One Suit" depends on luck and skill. Unless one cheats, it cannot be forced. Therefore, the "Pure One Suit" in mahjong can be called "Heavenly." In a corner of society, wherever people gather, if they use "artificial" means to create a "Pure One Suit," they must use mechanical means, and they also need to use handless squeezing and crowding to remove all the mixed colors, attracting "brothers-in-law," "cousins," "relatives," "fellow villagers," "neighbors," and so on. As long as they are from the same nest, they are all stuffed in, so that they can control everything with ease and teamwork. This is a "Pure One Suit" created by "artificial" means. This victory is even more impressive than the three points in mahjong, and it cannot be calculated in detail.

Cat's Eyes 185

— Yimin

When I was young, I read Qing Yu Quyuan's "Cat's Eyes" essay and learned that the cat's eyes change over time, with different shapes in the morning, evening, sunny, and rainy weather. If used to tell time, it is not accurate. Later, I verified this with the cats I kept at home, and it was true.

I am now excerpting some of the words from the essay to tell those who believe that cat's eyes can tell time:

"The anonymous 'Adjusting Types' of this dynasty has a 'Cat's Eyes Time-Telling Song' that says: 'A line at midnight and noon, round at mao and you, like ginkgo leaves at yin, shen, si, and hai, and like coins on their side at chen, xu, chou, and wei.'" I recorded this in the 'Tea Fragrance Studio Readings.'"

"Wang Mengwei said: 'The cat's eyes are bright at night but dim in the daytime. At noon, when the sunlight is strong, the cat's eyes are afraid of the sun and often close their eyes to sleep. Or if they open them, they are forced by the sunlight, and their eyes contract into a line. In the chen and si hours, the sun's power is not strong, and in the shen and you hours, the heat has already receded, so they all shrink like date pits. However, at night, they are round in all six hours. Only when viewed under a lamp do they also look like date pits, because they are afraid of the light. I remember one day a cat was lying on the desk, and it was exactly noon. I called it to the back porch to test it, and its eyes were only slightly thin. When I turned it to face the south window, it closed its eyes tightly, and when I pried them open, they immediately shrank into a line. Another day, the weather was gloomy with wind and rain, and it was also noon, but its eyes were still round. The same noon time but different due to sunny or rainy weather, the same day but different due to the brightness or darkness of the place. One can understand the principle. The ancients' song for telling time was based on what they saw and extrapolated to the night, but they never actually tested it in detail.'"

"According to my understanding, Mengwei's statement is quite reasonable. 'Youyang Miscellaneous Morsels' says: 'The cat's eyes are round in the morning and evening, and contract vertically like a thorn at noon.' So the ancients were indeed just speaking generally."

Recently, I saw Ba Lingjun's "Land Sundial of Life" article (see the previous "Children's Weekly"), which also says that cat's eyes can tell time. It is said with certainty, but it seems to be lying to children.

Anecdotes about Qihuang (Traditional Chinese Medicine) 186

— Yimei

Whether in cities or villages, in prosperous or remote places, there is no place where you cannot see a doctor's sign. Indeed, the relationship between medicine and human life is too close, with an inseparable connection. I usually have many interesting anecdotes about Qihuang, so I am recording them here to help with conversation.

Du Shan's Jin Xiaoyan was friends with the famous doctor Chuan Zhitin. Jin was poor and unable to support himself and loved orchids. Ting had dozens of pots of orchids in his garden. One winter, he was ill and unable to take care of himself, and the orchid buds that grew in the autumn were completely frozen and unable to open. Jin did not recover from his illness until the summer of the following year. One day, Fu came to see him and saw the frozen orchid buds in the garden still standing upright, not removed. He was touched and said to Xiaoyan: "You are in a difficult situation. Now there is a way to make you slightly richer." Jin asked him what it was. Fu said: "You should quickly collect all the frozen orchid buds in the garden. They are now dry and will not rot again. A certain official is greedy and unkind. His son is now ill and trusts me very much. He has taken several doses of medicine, and it will probably take a hundred doses to work. In the future, when I prescribe medicine, I will use frozen orchid buds as a medicinal guide. He will not be able to find them anywhere, and I can tell him that you have a collection and ask him to buy them. Ask for a high price, and he will not be stingy for the sake of his son." Later, a certain official did come to buy frozen orchid buds, at a price of two qian per bud, which was later increased to one tael of silver per bud. The last three buds were sold for ten taels of silver. In total, Jin earned more than ninety taels, which provided him with several months of food.

The imperial physician of Menghe treated Empress Dowager Cixi's illness. He first bribed the eunuch to see the prescriptions of the Imperial Hospital for several days. Ten out of ten were tonics. He knew the reason for the phlegm and shortness of breath. So he personally decocted the medicine and presented it to Cixi. After taking it, Cixi's condition improved day by day, and she rewarded him generously. He returned and said to his best friend: "What I gave was just radish juice."

Mr. Lu Tu'e is a novelist and a physician. Therefore, he often elaborates on the principles of medicine in his martial arts novels. Therefore, some people say that he medicalizes his novels. Recently, he edited and compiled "New Talk on National Medicine" for Xiaojing Mountain House. After it was published, he graciously sent me a copy. After reading it, I found it very interesting. It turned out that he was writing medical books using the method of writing novels, thus fictionalizing medicine. Tu'e excels at both, no wonder he can achieve such a wonderful combination of the two.

Zhang Family's Gossip and Li Family's Shortcomings 187

— Yiqiu

Little Western Paradise 188

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter Fifteen: Bitterly Earnest Advice Does Not Fall Flat, the Sound of Money and Shadows Sell People

I only heard Mrs. Hu say that this is not a business, and it's not very meaningful to talk about it every day. We are just repeating the first few sentences. Bei Hai's heart stirred, and he didn't want to leave. In the middle of the room, there was a skylight covered by an awning, with a long table in the middle, with several newspapers placed on it for people to read at will. Bei Hai turned his back to the window and leaned on the table to read the newspaper, taking the opportunity to listen to what they were saying. Jia Duocai continued, "It's not that I'm slow to act, it's because you're not efficient. That day, I was very happy and invited him to dinner. He rolled around in the mud and slept on Mr. Cheng's bed for half a day." Mrs. Hu interrupted, "Oh! What's the big deal, Mr. Cheng wasn't in the house." Jia Duocai said, "I don't care about that, why haven't I seen him since that day?" Mrs. Hu said, "Firstly, he's a little embarrassed about that day. Secondly, Master Jia has been very busy these past few days and is rarely at home, so he hasn't come." Jia Duocai said, "Even if what you say is reasonable, why isn't he here today?" Yang Huanhua said, "You should also forgive him. He's a young girl. It's always sitting in front of people and listening to others talk about his marriage. If things were settled with just one word, that would be fine. But no matter how much you talk about it, it's always unsuccessful. Think about it, it's always a bit embarrassing for a girl." Jia Duocai said, "What's embarrassing, he's slept naked on Mr. Cheng's bed. Now let's say a straight word, I can't manage his family. How much money does he want for his freedom? Mrs. Hu, go back and ask. If the price is not too high, we can naturally negotiate. If the price is too high, we'll end this matter and I won't care about it anymore." (245)

Fragrant Memories of Imperial Life 189

— Originally written by Princess Der Ling, translated by Qin Shouou

I pondered deeply, and it took me a long time to stop. When I raised my head, I happened to see the row of halls built on the side of Longevity Hill, so I remembered again! I thought: the metaphor I just made is really close to the truth. – Because those great palaces covered with yellow tiles can very well represent the Manchu Qing Empire. In fact, the Manchu Qing Empire is indeed the Empress Dowager's nanny; so she can now be regarded as a child playing on a boat, guarded by his nanny. However, this child is too precious, and in addition to this great nanny in spirit, there are also many teachers, tutors, and governesses to take care of her, so that she does not suffer any harm.

I was about to think again when the Empress Dowager finished her special lunch and said in a tone of admiration:

"Today, we can truly be said to be extremely happy!" She rinsed her mouth and said: "This suddenly reminded me of the words of our great sage Confucius, who said 'extreme joy is not permissible' and 'extreme joy produces sorrow'? Other ancient people also said that worries and joys often take turns to deal with people; so I think that after we have such excessive joy today, immediately, or in an hour, or later, tomorrow, perhaps that god of creation will inevitably tease us again!"

These words of hers, once sent into my eardrums, had a great impact, causing me to palpitate involuntarily, and I was worried that she would cause herself trouble; fortunately, she just said it orally and did not turn joy into sorrow. I think that her intention was probably because although she felt that this kind of concern was not without credibility, she also knew that such a relaxed and happy time was really not easy for her to obtain; so she had the idea of ​​living for the moment, and waiting for the god of creation to come up with some mystery tomorrow before dealing with it. (345)

Quick Sketches of the Cocoon Market 190

— (Meng Shuzu)

I. The usually quiet cocoon trade has suddenly become lively.

As usual, this scene should be exciting, comforting, and filled with smiling faces, whether from the seller or the buyer.

But this year, everything is an exception.

"A price of eighteen or nineteen yuan per 'dan' of cocoons, I'm not exaggerating, there's no profit to be had!" An old farmer with a face full of wrinkles grumbled. "I estimated these two baskets of cocoons would sell for six yuan and six jiao, but after arguing to the death, I only got five yuan and five jiao. Redeeming rice means I can't redeem clothes, and redeeming clothes means I can't redeem rice." Another person sighed and muttered to themselves.

The cocoon merchants are so anxious, lowering the price day after day, but the goods are still not being pushed. If they don't collect enough goods, they're sure to lose money. The clerks, who were originally the most arrogant, can't muster any energy in this atmosphere.

The most disappointed are the small food stalls on both sides. Only these few sell food to the cocoon sellers, and these few are so stingy. One by one, they walk past quickly, as if embarrassed, trying their best to avoid the stall owners' gaze.

Excitement, comfort, smiling faces – all have become a dream of the past, leaving no impression on this year's cocoon market. Sericulture has indeed failed.

Social Snapshot

A Murdered Woman (Part 1) 191

— You Aimei

In this era where suicide cases seem to increase daily, my cousin, Zhu Qingzhang, also hanged herself two months ago. This tragic news only reached me recently through a letter from my mother. My friendship with her was like that of siblings, so naturally, I felt extraordinary sorrow and couldn't help but shed tears. At the same time, I feel that her suicide is somewhat different from that of ordinary people because I know that she fell into an unfortunate situation due to the man-eating ethics and that she walked toward the path of demise because of the oppression of feudal society. Therefore, I believe that on the surface, she is a suicide victim, but in reality, she is a murdered one!

Her background is truly pitiful. Although she was born into a middle-class family with a passable life, the family was entirely structured like something out of the seventeenth century. Every man, woman, old and young, possessed a stubborn mind and a solemn face. To top it off, she lost her father early, leaving only a widowed mother who was kind and loving. As for the rest, whether it was her grandfather, grandmother, uncle, or aunt, she dared not say a word. Therefore, from a young age, she was confined in this ashen atmosphere, losing all her naturalness and vivacity, and developing a gentle temperament and a timid will. No matter what kind of embarrassment she suffered, she could only cry in secret to resolve it.

Even more unfortunate, not long after her father died, her mother began to cough up blood. Because her father suffered from lung disease, there was some suspicion that she had been infected. At that time, her mother moaned in bed, looking at her and her younger sister, thinking to herself, "If I fall ill and am unable to recover, leaving these two weak daughters behind, they will definitely not have a good life. It's better to make arrangements early and betroth them to families, considering it their path to survival." Under this thought, she hastily entrusted a matchmaker to betroth her to a Xu family in Linxi Village. Later, her mother did not die, and no one would have thought that this had created a major mistake regarding her life. Thus, the greatest tragedy of her life unfolded scene by scene:

Her husband, surnamed Xu, was a dandy from the countryside. He had not received a family education, resulting in a perverse temperament and improper behavior. After becoming an adult, his father once sent him to a middle school in Nanjing, but he dropped out in less than a year, so there was no way to talk about academics. However, he also had his specialties: eating, dressing, whoring, and gambling. He was proficient in all four areas. At that time, he had already become involved with a village girl and often made a scene in front of his mother, demanding to break off the engagement with his fiancée and marry his lover. Later, these rumors spread to her family. Her mother also regretted it very much. However, the society in Bao'ying upheld ancient morals, and the Zhu family was known for its literary tradition! Breaking off the engagement would be detrimental to social morals and shame the family. As for whether the boy was good or bad, it was not a problem. A chicken should follow a chicken, and a dog should follow a dog; besides, he was still a person, after all. Moreover, as long as her daughter had good luck, he would naturally become a good person after marrying into his family. Therefore, she tried her best to compromise. As a result, on the day of Qingming Festival, taking advantage of the bustling atmosphere of everyone following the tradition of strolling in Songgang, her mother pretended to take her out for a stroll, but secretly had the matchmaker lead her husband past them, pointing him out for him to see her appearance. As expected, her husband, because she was more beautiful than his lover, abandoned the village girl and eagerly set a date to marry her.

Fujian Province Discusses Methods for Implementing Compulsory Education 193

(Fuzhou Correspondence) The central task of education in Fujian Province for the 24th year of the Republic (i.e., starting in July of this year) has been defined as promoting compulsory education and implementing mandatory literacy. Recently, the Department of Education, as the new year is about to begin, convened a discussion meeting on the 17th for education administrative personnel of various counties. Attendees included Zheng Zhenwen, Director of the Department of Education; Xu Shifeng, Counselor of the Provincial Government; Zheng Tan, Zhu Hanchuan, and Tang Shouqian, Section Chiefs of the Department of Education; He Erong and Wang Shuxian, Supervisors; Weng Zaihao and Xue Yidan, Clerks; Zheng Zhensen, Chai Lian, and Wu Lianlian, Directors of the Compulsory Education Committee; and education section chiefs from various counties, totaling 76 people. After performing the formalities, Director Zheng reported the purpose of the meeting and the process of contacting the central government for compulsory education funding, stating that the national treasury would subsidize one-third, the provincial treasury would subsidize one-third, and the counties would raise one-third, totaling approximately 375,000 yuan annually. It is proposed to establish a provincial and county compulsory education committee to handle the matter. After the report, discussions began on (1) the draft implementation details for compulsory education, totaling sixteen articles. It was resolved that after the Ministry's "Provisional Outline for the Implementation of Compulsory Education Nationwide" is sent to the province, this provincial single-line method will be submitted to the Provincial Government for approval and promulgation; (2) the draft implementation details for compulsory education, totaling thirty articles. It was resolved that the 8th article regarding teacher qualifications, the 12th article regarding private schools, the 17th article regarding the adoption of a class-based teaching system in short-term primary schools, the 23rd article regarding the treatment of teachers in short-term primary schools, and the 28th article regarding penalties for compulsory enrollment of children should all be revised; (3) the estimation of the number of short-term primary schools in each county was discussed. It was resolved that the estimation would be made after each section chief returned to their county to investigate the number of out-of-school children; (4) the establishment of graduation standards for compulsory education and the holding of exams for exemption from education were discussed. It was resolved that because Article 26 of the draft implementation details for compulsory education already provides for exemption methods, this proposal would be reserved. In addition, regarding vocational education, (1) the organizational law of the county compulsory literacy committee, (2) the use of the baojia system to promote social and popular education, and regarding social education, the question of whether to continue or discontinue the popular schools that have already been established after the implementation of compulsory literacy education, were all discussed in detail. Subsequently, thirteen points regarding general local education administration to be paid attention to were reported: (1) reorganizing education funding, (2) hiring qualified teachers, (3) increasing the salaries of primary school teachers, (4) earnestly implementing the teaching of the national language, (5) emphasizing physical education and school hygiene, (6) holding scholarships for poor students, (7) planning vocational schools and supplementary schools, (8) county governments should cooperate with normal school districts to study the status of teachers and guide primary schools, (9) district offices should be used to handle education supervision and urge supervisors to conduct universal inspections, (11) rigorously implement primary school sampling tests, (12) report various statistics and school status reports on time, and (13) plan for children's equality. Finally, Supervisor Wang Shuxian raised five points that should be paid attention to in education in various counties: (1) pay attention to rural education, (2) fill enrollment quotas, (3) pay attention to the equipment of vocational schools, (4) study teaching methods, and (5) the number of schools should be evenly distributed. (June 19)

Ministry of Education Orders Improvement of Vocational Education in Fujian Province 198

The Ministry of Education issued an order on the 20th to the Department of Education of Fujian Province, stating that according to the report on the inspection of vocational education in the province submitted by Inspectors Dai Xia, Special Commissioner Sun Guofeng, the number of vocational schools in the province is too small, and the content is not substantial enough to meet the needs. The subjects offered do not pay attention to the improvement of local agricultural and industrial industries, and improvements should be made. Furthermore, the province's previous submission of the establishment and funding allocation methods for secondary schools in the 23rd year of the Republic still included plans to establish a Putian agricultural vocational school, which has not yet been implemented. Earnest planning and implementation should also be carried out to meet the establishment and funding allocation standards for secondary schools on schedule. The relevant points for improvement are listed below for compliance and reporting:

(1) The improvement of various industries in the province is urgently needed, but the establishment of existing vocational schools is not sufficient to meet the needs. The actual situation should be considered, and schools should be established in accordance with the standards promulgated by the Ministry, using provincial funds, and at the same time, cities and private secondary schools should be supervised to establish or reorganize schools. (2) Existing provincial vocational schools place too much emphasis on industry, and the civil engineering subject is in high demand due to highway construction. However, except for one agricultural school, all vocational schools have this subject, and the future career paths of students will inevitably become a problem. The actual situation of various civil engineering projects in the region should be used as a standard for training technical personnel in this area. (3) Provincial vocational schools of an industrial nature have generally failed to focus on improving and promoting local crafts. Efforts should be made to establish them within the realm of possibility. (4) The majority of people in the province are engaged in agriculture, and agricultural development is lagging behind. The training of agricultural vocational talent is an urgent task. However, besides the Putian agricultural vocational school, which is still under preparation, there is only one Fuzhou senior agricultural vocational school in the province, which is insufficient to meet the needs. The Putian vocational school should be strictly supervised to ensure earnest preparation and establishment. At the same time, the industrial situation in various regions should be considered, and agricultural vocational schools should be added as soon as possible. (5) Existing provincial vocational schools have different histories and generally offer a wide range of subjects. The department should reorganize them based on local needs, focusing on centralized management as a principle. (6) It is estimated that the province needs 20 senior vocational school teachers in both agriculture and industry. It is proposed to send students to study at universities abroad, but for the sake of convenience, domestic colleges and universities can also be entrusted to provide training. (7) The distribution of academic and practical courses in the curricula of a small number of vocational schools differs from the standards promulgated by the Ministry. Corrections should be made and earnestly implemented in accordance with the standards. (8) The Fuzhou Senior Agricultural Vocational School has rural courses and the equipment is not substantial. The school is located in the city and has little contact with the rural environment. Efforts should be made to relocate the school to the suburbs and improve the equipment to improve the efficiency of education. Graduates face considerable difficulty finding jobs and should be assisted. According to the school's plan, canning manufacturing and horticultural seedlings, etc., should be added, and the school has made considerable achievements in raising livestock in recent years. It seems that the scope of the agriculture and forestry courses can be reduced and the focus shifted to agricultural manufacturing and by-products. (9) The Fuzhou Industrial Vocational School is generally well-managed, and the equipment is impressive. However, it has been established for a long time, and there has been a slight lack of supplementation over the years. The budget should be used to increase equipment expansion costs as much as possible, and the content should be enriched as much as possible, with electrical engineering, machinery, and civil engineering as the foundation. The manufacturing factories should also pay attention to the production and marketing of common commodities on the market. (10) The Fuzhou Vocational School has a considerable foundation, but it offers industrial, commercial, household affairs, midwifery, and nursing courses, and there are an equal number of male and female students. The allocation of equipment and the implementation of moral education are more difficult. The number of courses should be reduced, and training should be centralized. (11) The Xiamen Vocational School offers commercial courses, which are well-suited to local needs. Efforts should be made to find more internship opportunities for students to increase their experience. If necessary, women's vocational courses such as household affairs and sewing can be added. (12) The private Hui'er Yuan has achieved good results in lacquer work and rattan work. In the future, the styles and structures should be further improved. This order is issued.

Jiangsu Department of Education Revises Methods for Training Primary School Teachers, and the List of Recommended Personnel from Each District Has Been Submitted to the Department 199

(Zhenjiang News) In order to train unqualified primary school teachers in each district, the Jiangsu Department of Education has designated training classes attached to the provincial normal schools in each normal school district according to actual needs. The counties have now submitted the names of those recommended for training. The second district has nine people from Wuxi, seven from Wujin, five from Yixing, three from Liyang, six from Jiangyin, two from Jingjiang, four from Jintan, two from Wuxian, five from Wujiang, and two from Changshu. The third district has two people from Taicang, eleven from Kunshan, four from Jiading, three from Shanghai, eight from Songjiang, four from Nanhui, six from Qingpu, three from Fengxian, five from Jinshan, two from Chuansha, one from Baoshan, and five from Chongming. The fourth district has four people from Huaiyin, four from Huaian, three from Siyang, eleven from Lianshui, six from Shuyang, eight from Suqian, one from Gaoyou, two from Baoying, and two from Funing. The fifth district has four people from Donghai, four from Tongshan, five from Fengxian, four from Pei County, five from Xiao County, four from Dangshan, four from Pi County, four from Suining, five from Guanyun, and six from Ganyu. The sixth district has three people from Rugao, nine from Nantong, six from Dongtai, three from Taixing, three from Taixian, four from Hai'an, two from Yancheng, eleven from Haimen, and four from Qidong. The revised interim measures for the training classes are excerpted as follows: Article 1. For the purpose of training unqualified primary school teachers in each district in Jiangsu Province, the Department of Education, in accordance with factual needs, has designated primary school teacher training classes of the first or second grade attached to provincial normal schools in each normal school district. The schools designated in the preceding paragraph shall follow these measures in conducting such classes. Article 2. The training period shall be limited to one academic year. Article 3. Each grade shall have a fixed number of 45 students, both male and female. Article 4. Students shall be between the ages of 18 and 26. Article 5. Students shall be recommended by the education bureaus or county governments of each county within each normal school district before the start of the academic year from among currently serving unqualified primary school teachers who have graduated from junior high school and have served for more than one year. The quota for each county shall be determined separately by the Department based on a survey of unqualified teachers. Article 6. Students shall be exempt from tuition, food, lodging, sports, and book fees during the training period. Article 7. These teacher training classes shall not admit self-funded students. Article 8. When the education bureaus or county governments of each county recommend students, they shall prepare two copies of the following resume form, one to be sent to the recommending school and one to be sent to the Department of Education for review. The resume form for recommended students shall include name, origin, gender, age, whether or not a member of the party, education experience, current school of service. Article 9. When recommended students arrive at the school, they shall submit their graduation certificate and current service certificate, which shall be secretly verified by the principal and reported to the Department of Education for record. Article 10. If it is found that the students recommended by the education bureaus or county governments of each county do not meet the qualifications stipulated in Article 5, in addition to expelling them from school and recovering all expenses from the original recommending agency, administrative penalties shall be imposed on the responsible personnel of the original recommending agency. Article 11. The curriculum of the training class shall apply the subjects and hours of the simplified normal department curriculum promulgated by the Ministry, but the goals are as follows: A. Goals: (1) Emphasis on the exploration of practical problems, (2) Basic training and professional training shall proceed simultaneously, (3) Must be integrated with the primary school curriculum, (4) Emphasis on the improvement of each subject and teaching methods. B. Curriculum Distribution Table: First Semester: Total teaching hours per week: 36 hours, including Chinese Language, Arithmetic, Geography, Education Psychology: 4 hours each, Introduction to Natural Education, Primary School Teaching Materials and Teaching Methods, Practical Training: 3 hours each, Physical Education, Labor, Drawing, and Music: 2 hours each. Total hours for extracurricular activities and self-study at school per week: 24 hours. Second Semester: Total teaching hours per week: 36 hours, including Chinese Language, Arithmetic, History, Primary School Teaching Materials and Teaching Methods: 4 hours each, Nature: 3 hours, Physical Education, Labor, Chinese Painting, Music, Primary School Administration: 2 hours each, Practical Training: 7 hours. Total hours for extracurricular activities and self-study at school per week: 24 hours. Article 12. Regarding the examination of grades, promotion, demotion, admission, and expulsion, as well as various reward and punishment measures, all shall be handled in accordance with the original measures of the school. Article 13. Students who complete their studies and pass the examination shall be granted a simplified normal department graduation certificate upon approval by the Department. Article 14. After unqualified teachers in each county are ordered to be transferred, their vacant positions shall be filled by normal school graduates dispatched by the education bureaus or county governments of each county and reported to the Department of Education for record. Article 15. After the training period for students is completed, the education bureaus or county governments of each county shall assign them to fill the vacancies of unqualified teachers in various schools in order of the list of those who are transferred. Article 16. These measures shall be revised by the Department of Education of Jiangsu Province and reported to the Ministry of Education and the Provincial Government for record and implementation.

Zhejiang Department of Education Promulgates Measures for the Examination of Vocational School Internships, Divided into Four Categories: Agriculture, Industry, Commerce, and Home Affairs 200

The Zhejiang Department of Education believes that internships in vocational schools are most important. Article 36 of the regulations for vocational schools promulgated by the Ministry stipulates that "internships should account for 50% in principle," and Article 41 stipulates that "the teaching of each subject in vocational schools should be based on the principle of practical training first and then lecturing." It can be seen that internships are extremely important in the curricula of vocational schools at all levels. Recently, it has been found that vocational schools at all levels have not paid much attention to internships, and there are no concrete examination measures for students' internship time on weekdays, so that the theory and practice learned by students cannot be combined, which has a profound impact on students' vocational skills. Therefore, the Zhejiang Department of Education has specially promulgated interim measures for the examination of vocational school internships, divided into four categories: agriculture, industry, commerce, and home affairs. Students who fail the internship examination shall not be allowed to graduate. A notice is issued to all city and county governments for compliance.

National Language Association Creates Blind Script and Sign Language; Initial Reading Approved; Awaiting Trial During Summer Before Requesting Ministry of Education to Issue Order for Adoption; Shanghai and Beijing Summer National Language Training Courses to Commence Next Month 204

The National Mandarin Education Promotion Association is sparing no effort in promoting Mandarin education. This year, the association has designated as the Mandarin Construction Year, actively carrying out construction work. Recently, it has created blind script and sign language, which has been initially approved by the association's committee. Details are as follows:

Creating Blind Script and Sign Language: Recognizing the lack of uniformity in written language teaching in schools for the blind and deaf nationwide, the association specifically entrusted officers in various regions to conduct detailed investigations. The types of scripts are extremely diverse, encompassing both Chinese and Western styles, deemed unsuitable. Therefore, a committee was specifically organized to compile blind script and sign language, and it was decided to conduct preliminary trials. It is planned to recruit a number of deaf students to teach sign language and a number of blind students to teach blind script during the summer vacation this year. If the results are excellent, a request will be submitted to the Ministry of Education to issue an order for adoption by blind and deaf schools nationwide, it is said.

Summer Training in National Language: In order to assist teachers and staff of elementary schools in the Shanghai Nanshi area in utilizing the summer vacation to study standard Mandarin, the association is specifically organizing summer Mandarin training courses in both locations. The curriculum is divided into three types: phonetic symbols, Mandarin Romanization, and basic Mandarin speaking, emphasizing skills. Tuition fees will not be charged. It is reported that the Shanghai course will commence on July 10th, and the Nanjing course will commence on July 11th, lasting for five weeks.

Elementary School Speech Contest: The association is scheduled to hold the Hankou Elementary School Students Speech Contest at the Hankou Civic Education Center on the 23rd of this month. The Hankou Municipal Government has already issued an order to students from public and private elementary schools throughout the city to participate in four groups. The judges invited include Dan Chengyi, Mei Gongren, and Wu Shaoshu, standing committee members of the Municipal Party Department; Du Jixiang, section chief of the Municipal Government; Shen Danjie, division chief; inspectors Wang Zhaojun, Xia Shengang, Luo Yian, Han Chang, and other party and government personnel; as well as vocational high school principals and Mandarin experts, who will serve as judges for each group.

School News 210

Zhonghua Vocational School: The Xiaoximen Zhonghua Vocational School has two departments, industry and commerce. The industrial department is divided into mechanical and civil engineering. There is a mechanical practice workshop in the school. Other facilities such as surveying instruments, architectural specimens, and models are well-equipped. More than a thousand graduates have served in society. The school's business department has always accepted female students. It is now reported that the industrial department will also accept female students starting from this summer. In Europe and the United States, it is very common for women to study and serve in mechanical and civil engineering technical work, but in our country, it is still an innovation. From now on, it can greatly increase the opportunities for women in our country to serve and employ, promote equality between men and women, and especially promote the important initiative of industrial culture in our country, opening up the depressing atmosphere of recent years. In the midst of this national crisis, it is a good phenomenon.

Qingnian Middle School: Xiafei Road Qingnian Middle School has been running a summer school every summer vacation as usual. This is the ninth session. In the past eight sessions, the total number of students who came to the school for tutoring has exceeded two thousand five hundred. Because the school has spacious buildings and is adjacent to the French Park, it is very suitable for summer vacation. If you want to stay at the school during the summer vacation, the cost of food and accommodation is only 20 yuan. The teachers in charge of the various subjects are also well-known people. In terms of academics, courses are set up in Chinese, English, arithmetic, geometry, algebra, trigonometry, physics, and chemistry, and classes are scheduled to begin on July 8th. Prospectus available upon request.

Huzhong Summer School: The Huzhong Summer Tutoring School on Fada Road, Dongxin Bridge in this city was founded by graduates from various universities in the country. It uses the summer vacation to tutor all courses for the entrance exams to universities and middle schools, including Chinese, English, Japanese, French, mathematics, party principles, and shorthand. Classes are scheduled to begin on July 8th.

Minsheng Elementary and Middle School: The Minsheng Elementary and Middle School Summer Tutoring School in Kaibei, this city, is scheduled to start classes on July 8th. The time is from 8:00 am to 11:00 am every morning. The tutoring subjects are Chinese, English, arithmetic, and general knowledge. The tuition fee for the junior high school department is only 2.5 yuan, 2 yuan for the senior grades of the elementary school department, 1.5 yuan for the middle grades, and 1 yuan for the lower grades.

Sports News

Guangdong Province Attends the National Games; Methods for Training Athletes; Initial Selection of Athletes in Various Sports Completed; Training Steps Divided into Three Periods 212

In order to prepare for participating in this year's Double Tenth National Games, the Guangdong Provincial Sports Association has recently actively held initial selections and engaged in training, so that they can come to Shanghai to participate at that time. The basic track and field team members have been selected and started training at the Provincial Public Sports Ground on the 17th. The training time is scheduled for Mondays and Thursdays from 4:30 pm to 6:00 pm. As for the ball team members, they have also been selected in turn in recent days. The count is as follows: football, 7 police team members, 11 air force team members, 2 Sun Yat-sen University members, 4 Lingnan University members, 2 tennis members from the Civic Sports Association, 2 Sun Yat-sen University members, 2 individual members; men's basketball, 5 Pui Ching Middle School members, 3 Sun Yat-sen University members, 4 Aviation School members, 2 Lingnan University members, 1 member each from the 7th and 8th Divisions, 2 members from the National Academy of Sciences; women's basketball, 6 Guangzhou Girls' Middle School members, 3 Guangzhou Women's Normal School members, 2 Jiaozhong Middle School members, 1 member each from Xiangqin University and Sun Yat-sen University, 6 Shantou City members, 2 Zhixin School members; men's volleyball, 6 Physical Education School members, 5 Pui Ying Middle School members, 6 Sun Yat-sen University members, 1 member each from Xiangqin University and the Gendarmerie Headquarters, 1 member each from the 7th and 8th Divisions, 1 Taishan Normal School member; women's basketball, 7 Sun Yat-sen University members, 5 Guangzhou Women's Normal School members, 5 Guangzhou Girls' Middle School members, 1 member each from National University, Jiaozhong University, Zhixin Girls' School, Peizhi Girls' School, Jiefang Girls' Middle School, 1 member from Zhongshan County.

The Provincial Department of Education has already hired more than ten sports experts from the province to serve as members of the preparatory committee for participating in the National Games and established the preparatory committee. The committee is divided into a training department and an administrative department, responsible for preparing for participation and training matters. The training agency is divided into track and field, volleyball, basketball, softball, tennis, swimming, national arts, table tennis, and football groups, each with a group leader and several instructors. The training period is divided into three phases: the first phase is in June and July of this year, with two training sessions per week for each type; the second phase is in August, selecting formal representatives, organizing training camps, and training together; the third phase is in September, with three training sessions per week for each type. The training venues are divided into three locations: tennis training is at the Civic Sports Association, swimming training is at the Dongshan Water Sports Association, and a training camp is set up at Lingnan University. In addition to the above three locations, the remaining training locations are all at the Dadong Road Public Sports Ground. At the end of the first training phase, the training department will select a number of people from the basic team members as formal representatives to attend the 6th National Games and must immediately join the training camp to receive the second and third phases of training. The training camp is the organization for the second phase of training for the basic team, and the time is set for one month. The food and accommodation expenses of the athletes receiving training are all provided by the camp. In the camp, practice techniques twice each morning and afternoon, listen to lectures for one hour in the morning, and hold hiking trips or recreational activities in the afternoon (June 15).

Commercial News

Finance Flourishing Sentiment, Gold Bar Premium Exceeds 80 Yuan 219

The gold market, stable then firm yesterday, broke through the 80-yuan mark, thoroughly stirring up strong buying sentiment, with the public mood extremely robust. Rumors spread within the market, suggesting a particularly favorable trend. Despite continuous reports of increases in Indian silver, sentiment remained unmoved. In the morning, influenced by the overseas silver market, with declines in both the UK and US, traders claimed that the US would increase by .0625 after the market closed, making large purchases, and that there were some transactions above the closing price of 1.25, causing some selling. In the London forward silver market, declines ranged from 3.5 to 5.7 percent. Exchange rate fluctuations were minimal. London raw gold fell 2.5 pence. Reports stated that American bankers would force the government to implement silver policies, but these floated psychologically and failed to rally. Outside the market, pre-market trading opened, with sellers eager at 80 yuan, quickly dropping to 77-78 yuan before stabilizing slightly, then rising to around 80 yuan and becoming steady. After opening, the Central Bank announced its rates, with both the UK and US unchanged and Customs Gold Units falling by 0.2 percent. The standard gold bar premium listed by the bank dropped to 836.3 yuan, and sentiment flagged slightly. Banks were willing to release and lower the price. It was anticipated that the Hongkong and Shanghai Banking Corporation (HSBC) would announce unchanged rates for both the UK and US, having little impact. Subsequently, the exchange rate market hardened, dropping once, but buyers took advantage of the low prices. Soon, it returned to stability, and demand gradually became mediocre, and the market situation became stagnant again. The banks’ buying appetite gradually revived, allowing the buying side to maintain strong support. Finally, both the Hong Kong and Shanghai markets softened, stirring up a buying wave. After breaking through the 80-yuan barrier, short sellers scrambled to cover, and the trend was firm at noon. In the afternoon market, although Indian silver rose by 6.7 annas, it lacked much downward pressure, and sentiment was unusually robust. Buying sentiment was particularly strong, and soon the market trended upward again. Banks and brokers rushed to sell US dollars, rallying after falling back but mostly fluctuating. Later, when Indian silver rose another 2 annas, there was still little downward pressure and strong support. The Central Bank, etc., found it difficult to raise prices again, so in the end, the bulls sold off slightly, causing a slight drop. Swaps were still posted by the short side at around 1.5 yuan yesterday. Here is a record of the day's market conditions:

The morning opened at 779.3 yuan, up 1.4 yuan from the previous closing. The Central Bank announced its rates, with Customs Gold Units falling by 0.2 percent, and prices gradually dropped from 9.7 yuan. Traders like Dada, Fuxing, Yongda, Decheng, Hengyu, and Hengchang sold off, retreating to 8 yuan. Fuxing, Yongqian, Changxiang, Chunyuan, Yongyuan, and Changyong took delivery at the low, rising to 9.5 yuan. It was anticipated that HSBC would announce unchanged rates for both the UK and US, and the market fluctuated. The highest price during the day was 784.6 yuan, and the lowest was 777.5 yuan, a fluctuation of 7.1 yuan. The result was a further increase of 4.3 yuan compared to the previous closing.

The closing price for the standard Central Bank gold bar premium listed decreased to 836.3 yuan, which, according to the closing price, was around 54 yuan, down more than 5 yuan from the previous closing. Overnight Interest Rate Exceeds 20% 221

Silver Dollar Fluctuations: Copper Coins Increase by 2,500 222

Yesterday, the silver dollar market's improving momentum was propelled by the upcoming conclusion of the first half of the year for banks, necessitating clear settlement of transactions between institutions. The market interest rate for silver dollars exceeded 20%, reaching 22% in the morning and afternoon, a 2% increase from the previous day. However, the availability of funds appeared slightly weaker than before. The market opened at a slightly lower rate of 20%, settling at 50%. Due to limited funds, it rebounded by 10%, settling at 60%. Nonetheless, this was a 10% decrease from the previous day's market. Swap transactions amounted to over 1.4 million in the morning and over 200,000 in new transactions. There were no afternoon transactions. The total clearing was approximately 1.2 million. Dollar mortgages redeemed were over 200,000, with new mortgages made totaling over 300,000. 700,000 bank notes were collected, 500,000 banknotes were issued, 700,000 coded banknotes were transacted, 400,000 remittances were received, 150,000 from brokers was received, and 200,000 left the bank. Banks' receipt and disbursement reports showed that foreign banks collected over 2.5 million in bill payments, over 3.1 million in miscellaneous receipts such as goods mortgages, over 400,000 in special remittances, over 900,000 in foreign exchange settlements, and 100,000 was taken out of warehouses. Chinese banks collected over 2.8 million in bill payments, over 3.8 million in miscellaneous receipts such as goods mortgages, over 500,000 in special remittances, over 700,000 in foreign exchange settlements, and 100,000 were warehoused. Japanese banks collected over 2.3 million in bill payments, over 3.3 million in miscellaneous receipts such as goods mortgages, over 300,000 in special remittances, over 600,000 in foreign exchange settlements, and equal amounts were taken in and out. Qianzhuang foreign exchange contracts cleared over 34 million, and foreign exchange head payments cleared over 4.4 million. Yesterday, Jiangnan small dollars rose to 4 yuan in the morning, reaching 835 yuan, then decreased by 2 yuan in the afternoon, settling at 833 yuan. Morning transactions totalled 6,000 jiao, while afternoon transactions totalled 1,000 jiao.
